  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  // By definition of DotProduct, we have
  // DotProduct(a', b') = DotProduct(a, b) + a'[*] * b'[*]
  // where a'[*] = a[|a|-1] and b'[*] = b[|b|-1].

  assert a[|a|-1] == x;
  assert b[|b|-1] == y;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]

  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {

  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{

  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert ValidSolution(a, b);
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  // a'[..|a'|-1] equals a
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  // b'[..|b'|-1] equals b
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

    }

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]); // This proves DotProduct(a[..i+1], b+[a[i+1]]) == DotProduct(a[..i], b) + a[i]*a[i+1]
      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]); // This proves DotProduct(a[..i+1], b+[-a[i-1]]) == DotProduct(a[..i], b) + a[i]*(-a[i-1])
      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  // The definition of DotProduct follows the recursive structure,
  // so the assertion holds by unfolding DotProduct and using the
  // inductive hypothesis.
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      // Append a[i+1] to b and maintain the dot product property
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      // Append -a[i-1] to b and maintain the dot product property
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  assert DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y by {
    // Proof by induction on |a|
    if |a| == 0 {
      // Base case: a and b are empty
      assert DotProduct([], []) == 0 by {
        // By definition of DotProduct
        assert DotProduct([], []) == 0;
      }
      assert DotProduct([x], [y]) == x * y by {
        // By definition of DotProduct
        assert DotProduct([x], [y]) == x * y;
      }
      assert 0 + x * y == DotProduct([x], [y]) by {
        assert 0 + x * y == x * y;
      }
    } else {
      // Inductive step: |a| > 0
      var a' := a[..|a|-1];
      var b' := b[..|b|-1];
      assert DotProduct(a, b) == DotProduct(a', b') + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1] by {
        // By definition of DotProduct
        assert DotProduct(a, b) == DotProduct(a', b') + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1];
      }
      assert DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a', b') + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1] + x * y by {
        // By definition of DotProduct
        assert DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct((a + [x])[..|a + [x]|-1], (b + [y])[..|b + [y]|-1]) + (a + [x])[|a + [x]|-1] * (b + [y])[|b + [y]|-1];
        assert (a + [x])[..|a + [x]|-1] == a;
        assert (b + [y])[..|b + [y]|-1] == b;
        assert (a + [x])[|a + [x]|-1] == x;
        assert (b + [y])[|b + [y]|-1] == y;
        assert DotProduct(a, b) + x * y == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
      }
      assert DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y by {
        // Combine previous equalities
        assert DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a', b') + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1] + x * y;
        assert DotProduct(a, b) == DotProduct(a', b') + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1];
        assert DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
      }
    }

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  // The postcondition follows from the definition of DotProduct
  // and the fact that the appended elements are x and y.
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      // Append a[i] to the dot product
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      // Append -a[i-1] to the dot product
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      assert i + 1 < |a|; // because |a| is even and i < |a|
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      assert i - 1 >= 0; // because i is odd and > 0
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a'[..|a'|-1], b'[..|b'|-1]) == DotProduct(a, b);
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a'[..|a'|-1], b'[..|b'|-1]) + a'[..|a'|-1][|a'|-1] * b'[..|b'|-1][|b'|-1];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1][|a'|-1] == x;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1][|b'|-1] == y;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)

    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|

  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}
